###########################
# News Events	#
############################
add_namespace = CW_Expansion_country
add_namespace = CW_Expansion_news


# Churchill delivers Iron Curtain speech
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.1
	title = CW_Expansion_country.1.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country1
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		date > 1946.3.4
		date < 1947.1.1
		SOV = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		NOT = {
			ENG = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		country_exists = SOV
		country_exists = ENG
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory}
	}
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.1.a
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.1
			hours = 6
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

#League of Nations Dissolved
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.3
	title = CW_Expansion_country.3.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country3
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1946.4.19
		date < 1947.1.1
		country_exists = UNA
		tag = UNA
	}
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.3.a
		if = { 
			limit = {
				country_exists = LON
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 892
				}
				transfer_state = 1111
			}
		
		}
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.3
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

# Italy abolishes monarchy
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.4
	title = CW_Expansion_country.4.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country4
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1946.7.12
		date < 1947.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_government = fascism
		}
		tag = ITA
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
	}
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.4.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.5
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.4
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = CW_Expansion_country.4.b
		add_popularity = { 
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -0.5
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = medium_decrease }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = medium_decrease }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = medium_decrease }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = large_decrease }
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = democratic
				size = 0.3
				    states = {
				115 156 991 992 117 2 157
				}
				}
	}	
}

# Soviet Union Rejects US Atomic-Energy Control plan
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.7
	title = CW_Expansion_country.7.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country7
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1947.3.4
		date < 1948.1.1
		country_exists = USA
		country_exists = SOV
		SOV = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		NOT = {
			USA = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		tag = USA
	}
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		RON_decrease_nuclear_spending = yes
		USA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.126
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.7.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		RON_increase_nuclear_spending = yes
		add_stability = -0.05
		USA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.127
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.7
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

# Tokyo Trials
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.9
	title = CW_Expansion_country.9.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country9
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1946.1.19
		date < 1947.1.1
		OR = {
			JAP = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			JAP = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = JAP
			}
		}
		OR = {
			tag = JAP
			AND = {
				tag = USA
				NOT = { country_exists = JAP } 
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
	}
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.9.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = USA
			}
		add_stability = 0.05
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
			}
		add_stability = -0.05
		}
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.9
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

# Juan PerÃ³n elected in Argentina
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.10
	title = CW_Expansion_country.10.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country10
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = "Peron Won"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.5
			}
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Juan Domingo Peron"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/ARG/Portrait_ARG_Juan_Domingo_Peron.dds"
			ideology = peronism
			traits = {
				nationalist_symbol
			}
		}
 		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.10
			hours = 6
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = ARG
	}
	option = {
		name = "The Ruling Party Won"
		
		trigger = {
		NOT = { has_government = fascism }
		is_puppet = no
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
			
	}
}

# USA Tests Nuclear Weapons
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.16
	title = CW_Expansion_country.16.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country16
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		date > 1946.7.1
		date < 1947.1.1
		tag = USA
		has_tech = nukes
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.16.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		add_tech_bonus = {
			bonus = 0.25
			uses = 1
			category = nuclear
		}
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.200
				hours = 6
			}
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.16
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

		}

			}
		add_stability = -0.05
		}

		}

		}
		
		RON_increase_health_spending = yes

			hours = 6
		}
	}

#Treaty of Brussels
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.49
	title = CW_Expansion_country.49.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.49.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country49
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#trigger = {
	#	NOT = {
	#		has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory
	#	}
	#	date > 1948.3.17
	#	date < 1959.1.1
	#	NOT = { country_exists = EUR }
	#	tag = BEL
	#	has_start_date > 1950.1.1
	#}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.49.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_government = democratic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		
		EUR = {transfer_state = 1113 }
		add_ideas = RON_European_Union
		
		}
		
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.49
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.49.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_government = communism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
	}
}

#Marshall_Plan
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.50
	title = CW_Expansion_country.50.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.50.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country50
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.50.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		
		add_ideas = { RI_marshall_plan_giver }
		
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					RON_is_European_Country = yes
					NOT = { has_government = communism }
					NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ron_diplomatic.238
					days = 1
				}
			}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.50
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.50.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
	}
}

	title = CW_Expansion_country.54.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.54.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country54
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory
		}
		date > 1948.6.24
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = SOV
		DDR = { is_subject_of = SOV }
		country_exists = DDR
		country_exists = GER
		country_exists = USA
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.54.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_threat = 10
		
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = USA
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.203
				hours = 6
			}
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.54
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.54.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		add_war_support = -0.10
		
	}
}

#War_Crimes_Trial
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.60
	title = CW_Expansion_country.60.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.60.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country60
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		date > 1948.11.12
		date < 1949.6.1
		OR = {
			JAP = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			JAP = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = JAP
			}
			NOT = {
				CHI = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			tag = JAP
			AND = {
				tag = USA
				NOT = { country_exists = JAP } 
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.60.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = USA
			}
		add_stability = 0.05
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
			}
		add_stability = -0.05
		}
		
		set_global_flag = JAP_Warcrimes_Trial

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.60
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

#War_Criminals_Executed
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.63
	title = CW_Expansion_country.63.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.63.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country63
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		date > 1948.12.23
		date < 1949.6.1
		OR = {
			JAP = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			JAP = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = JAP
			}
		}
		OR = {
			tag = JAP
			AND = {
				tag = USA
				NOT = { country_exists = JAP } 
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
		has_global_flag = JAP_Warcrimes_Trial
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.63.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = USA
			}
		add_stability = 0.05
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
			}
		add_stability = -0.05
		}
		
		clr_global_flag = JAP_Warcrimes_Trial

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.63
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

	desc = CW_Expansion_country.70.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		country_exists = CAN
		owns_state = 331
		owns_state = 332
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.70.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		CAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.126
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		
		CAN = {
			transfer_state = 331
			transfer_state = 332
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.70
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.70.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				CAN = {
					country_event = {
						id = ron_diplomatic.127
						hours = 6
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				ENG = { 
					country_event = {
						id = ron_decolonizationcountry.162
						hours = 6
					}
				}
				CAN = {
					country_event = {
						id = ron_diplomatic.1270
						hours = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		
		

		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.71
	title = CW_Expansion_country.71.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.71.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country71
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.71.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		
		create_faction = "NATO"
		every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = { 
						tag = BEL
						tag = CAN
						tag = DEN
						tag = FRA
						tag = ICE
						tag = ITA
						tag = LUX
						tag = HOL
						tag = NOR
						tag = POR
						tag = ENG
					}
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = generic.5
					hours = 1
				}
			}
		
		add_war_support = 0.10

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.71
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.71.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
		
	}
}

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		USA = { has_government = democratic }
		country_exists = SOV
		SOV = { has_government = communism }
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.82.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		add_stability = -0.05

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.82
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.82.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		add_stability = 0.05

	}
}

#warsaw_pact_sign
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.85
	title = CW_Expansion_country.85.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.85.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country85
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.85.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		
		create_faction = "Warsaw Pact"
		every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = { 
						tag = ALB
						tag = BUL
						tag = CZE
						tag = DDR
						tag = HUN
						tag = POL
						tag = ROM
					}
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = generic.5
					hours = 1
				}
			}
		
		add_war_support = 0.10

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.85
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.85.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
		
	}
}

# People's Republic of Albania Declared
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.86
	title = CW_Expansion_country.86.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.86.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country86
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ALB
		date > 1946.1.11
		date < 1947.1.1
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
		OR = {
			has_government = communism
			AND = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_puppet = no
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.86.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.5
			}
		}
		
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Enver Hoxha"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/ALB/Portrait_ALB_Enver_Hoxha.dds"
			ideology = hoxhaism
			traits = {
				staunch_stalinist
			}
		}

		add_stability = 0.05

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.86
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "We Will Not Allow This"
		
		trigger = {
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
		is_subject = no
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = communism
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ALB
						has_government = communism
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Enver Hoxha"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/ALB/Portrait_ALB_Enver_Hoxha.dds"
						ideology = hoxhaism
						traits = {
							staunch_stalinist
						}
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.25
				}
			}
		}
			
	}
}

# Charles de Gaulle Resigns
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.87
	title = CW_Expansion_country.87.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.87.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country87
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		date > 1946.1.20
		date < 1947.1.1
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Charles De Gaulle"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.87.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			last_election = "1949.1.1"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = 75
			communism = 25
		}
		
		retire_character = FRA_charles_de_gaulle
		
		#Should be Felix Gouin, but I don't have a portrait for him, so we will use Vincent Auriol temporarily
		
		FRA_vincent_auriol = {
			promote_character = {
				Ideology = democratic_socialism
			}
		}

		add_stability = -0.05

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.87
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

# Iran Gets Released by Soviets
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.88
	title = CW_Expansion_country.88.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.88.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country88
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1946.1.22
		date < 1947.1.1
		
		OR = {
			tag = PER
			AND = {
				tag = SOV
				NOT = { country_exists = PER } 
				owns_state = 1086
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.88.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = PER } 
			}
			set_global_flag = PER_Needs_Army
		}
		
		ENG = {
			release = PER
			end_puppet = PER
		}
		SOV = {
			release = PER
			end_puppet = PER
		}
		PER = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PER
					OR = { 
						is_owned_by = ENG 
						is_owned_by = SOV 
					}
				}
				PER = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PER_Needs_Army
			}
			PER = {
				load_oob = "PER_1940"
				set_country_flag = RON_Iranian_Civil_War
				clr_global_flag = PER_Needs_Army
			}
		}
		
		if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
		}
		PER = {
			start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					ideology = communism
					size = 0.3
					capital = 419
					states = { 419 420 1086 }
				}
			}
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.88
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

			factor = 10
		}
		
		release = PER
		end_puppet = PER

		add_stability = 0.05

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.91
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "We Won't Withdraw"
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				PER = { is_subject = no }
				PER = { is_subject_of = ENG }
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		
		add_political_power = -300
		
		if = {
			limit = {
			PER = { is_subject = no }
			}
			PER = {
				country_event = {
					id = ron_decolonizationdiplo.2
					hours = 1
				}
			}
		}

		add_stability = -0.05
	}

# Communist Victory In Czechoslovakia
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.96
	title = CW_Expansion_country.96.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country96
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CZE
		date > 1946.5.26
		date < 1947.1.1
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
		OR = {
			has_government = communism
			AND = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_puppet = no
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.96.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				communism = 55
				democratic = 45
			}
		}
		
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Klement Gottwald"
			desc = "POLITICS_KLEMENT_GOTTWALD_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Czech_Klement_Gottwald.dds"
			ideology = stalinism
		}

		add_stability = 0.05

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.96
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "We Will Not Allow This"
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
			is_subject = no
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = communism
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = CZE
						has_government = communism
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Klement Gottwald"
						desc = "POLITICS_KLEMENT_GOTTWALD_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Czech_Klement_Gottwald.dds"
						ideology = stalinism
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.25
				}
			}
		}
			
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.101
	title = CW_Expansion_country.101.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.101.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country101
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = BUL
		date > 1946.9.8
		date < 1947.1.1
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
		OR = {
			has_government = communism
			AND = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_puppet = no
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "Proclaim People's Republic"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				communism = 100
			}
		}
		
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Georgi Dimitrov"
			desc = "POLITICS_GEORGI_DIMITROV_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Bulgaria_Georgi_Dimitrov.dds"
			ideology = leninism
		}

		add_stability = 0.05

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.101
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "We Will Not Allow This"
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
			is_subject = no
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = communism
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = CZE
						has_government = communism
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Georgi Dimitrov"
						desc = "POLITICS_GEORGI_DIMITROV_DESC"

					}

			}

				}
			}
		}
			
	}

# Greek Communist Civil War
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.104
	title = CW_Expansion_country.104.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.104.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country104
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GRE
		date > 1946.3.30
		date < 1947.1.1
		has_civil_war = no
		NOT = { has_war_with = GRC }
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Crush Communism"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
		}

		GRC = { 
		transfer_state = 731
		transfer_state = 976
		load_oob = "GRC_1949"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = GRE
			type = civil_war
			}
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.104
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Support The Communists"
		
		trigger = { 
			is_subject = no
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.5
			}
		}
		
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Nikos Zachariadis"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/GRC/CW/Communist_Greece_Nikos_Zachariadis.dds"
			ideology = stalinism
		}
		
		
	}
}

		tag = CHI

		date < 1950.6.1
		surrender_progress > 0.49
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.158.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		CHI = {
			set_capital = {state = 524}
		}

		
	}
	option = {
		name = "Not Needed"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		
	}
}

# Treaty of The Hague
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.159
	title = CW_Expansion_country.159.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.159.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country159
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = HOL
		
		has_war_with = INS
		INS = { surrender_progress < 0.50 }
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.159.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		white_peace = INS
		
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = HOL }
			white_peace = INS
		}
		
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = INS }
			white_peace = HOL
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.159
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Truce"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.20
		add_stability = -0.20
		add_political_power = -200
		
	}
}

# India Becomes A Republic
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.172
	title = CW_Expansion_country.172.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.172.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country172
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = IND
			tag = RAJ
		}
		date > 1950.1.26
		date < 1951.1.1
		is_subject = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.172.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RAJ
			}
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = IND
		}

		add_stability = 0.10

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.172
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

# Last Kuomintang Troops Surrender In Mainland China
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.173
	title = CW_Expansion_country.173.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.173.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country173
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_war_with = PRC
		CHI = { surrender_progress > 0.8 }
		date > 1950.1.31
		date < 1951.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = weliveinthecursedtimeline
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.173.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
					if = { limit = { is_ai = no }
				hidden_effect = {
					TWN = { change_tag_from = CHI }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				TWN = { inherit_technology = CHI }
				TWN = {
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = democratic
						name = CHI_neutrality_party
						long_name = CHI_neutrality_party
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = neutrality
						name = CHI_neutrality_party
						long_name = CHI_neutrality_party
					}
					add_research_slot = 2
				}
			}
			TWN = {
				set_country_flag = weliveinthecursedtimeline
				transfer_state = 524
			}
				news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.158
			hours = 6
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "Keep Fighting"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.20
		add_stability = -0.20
		add_political_power = -200
		

	}
}

# Polish Expulsion of Ethnic Germans
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.177
	title = CW_Expansion_country.177.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.177.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country177
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = POL
		date > 1950.3.3
		date < 1951.1.1
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RON_Axis_Victory }
		NOT = { is_subject_of = GER }
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.177.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		POL = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = POL
					is_core_of = GER
				}
				POL = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				remove_core_of = GER
			}
		}

		add_manpower = -155495
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = DDR
			}
			DDR = {
				country_event = {
					id = DNC_Diplomacy.203
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = GER
				NOT = { country_exists = DDR }
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = DNC_Diplomacy.203
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.177
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "An Eye For An Eye Leaves The World Blind"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		
	}
}

# Belgian Monarchy Referendum
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.178
	title = CW_Expansion_country.178.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.178.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country178
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = BEL
		date > 1950.3.13
		date < 1951.1.1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Continue With The Monarchy"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 90
				communism = 5
				fascism = 5
			}
		}
		
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Leopold III"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/BEL/Portrait_Belgium_Leopold_III.dds"
			ideology = despotism
			traits = {
				stout_defender
			}
		}

		add_stability = 0.05

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.178
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "We Will Not Allow This"
		
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 90
				communism = 5
				fascism = 5
			}
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Paul-Henri Spaak"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/BEL/CW/Belgium_Paul-Henri_Spaak.dds"
				ideology = socialism
			}
			
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = BEL
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Leopold III"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/BEL/Portrait_Belgium_Leopold_III.dds"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							stout_defender
						}
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
			}
			}
			
		}
	}

			id = CW_Expansion_news.179
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "The Suez Is Rightfully British"
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_political_power = -100
		
		EGY = {
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.127
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.179

		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.187
	title = CW_Expansion_country.187.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.187.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country187
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SAF
		date > 1950.6.26
		date < 1951.1.1
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Suppress Communism"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		add_stability = 0.05
		
		add_popularity = {
			popularity = -0.30
			ideology = communism
		}
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.205
				hours = 6
			}
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.187
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Actually We Sympathize With Communism"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				communism > 0.29
			}
		}
		
		add_stability = -0.05

		add_popularity = {
			popularity = 0.30
			ideology = communism
		}
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.204
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		

	}
}

# Defense of South Korea
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.188
	title = CW_Expansion_country.188.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.188.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country188
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		date > 1950.6.27
		date < 1952.1.1
		ROK = { has_war_with = DPK }
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = MARPAC_voting_in_process
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = "Declare War on North Korea"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				threat < 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				#Not worth the risk if We are already at War with a major
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				#Not worth the risk if we are losing the war
				ROOT = {
					surrender_progress > 0.05
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = marpac.80
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -100

		declare_war_on = {
			target = DPK
			type = annex_everything
		}
		
		set_global_flag = KCW_American_Intervention

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.188
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Military Aid Will Suffice"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		#Symbolizes US Manpower Sent To Korea
		add_manpower = -326863
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -50000
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = 50
		
		ROK = {
			country_event = {
				id = DNC_Diplomacy.204
				hours = 6
			}
			division_template = {
   				name = "American Troops"
    			is_locked = yes
    			priority = 1
    			template_counter = 0
    			regiments = {
    			    infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
    			    infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
    			    infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
    			    infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
    			}

				#equivalent to 10k soldiers

			}
			
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { num_div = 1 }
				while_loop_effect= {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { num_div < 36}
					}

					create_unit = {
    					division = "name = \"American Troops\" division_template = \"American Troops\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
    					owner = ROK		
					}
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_div = 1 }
				}
			}

		}
		
		set_global_flag = KCW_American_Intervention

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.188
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Better Not Get Involved"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 8
				has_idea = foreign_neutral
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 8
				has_idea = neutrality_idea
			}
		}
		
		add_war_support = -0.10
		add_stability = 0.10
		add_political_power = 100

	}
}

# Chinese Intervention In Korean War
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.206
	title = CW_Expansion_country.206.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.206.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country206
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#trigger = {
	#	tag = PRC
	#	date > 1950.10.19
	#	date < 1952.1.1
	#	ROK = { has_war_with = DPK }
	#	has_government = communism
	#}

	option = {
		name = "Declare War on South Korea"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = KCW_American_Intervention }
					threat < 0.50
				}
				NOT = { USA = { has_war_with = ROK } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				#Not worth the risk if We are already at War with a major
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				#Not worth the risk if we are losing the war
				ROOT = {
					surrender_progress > 0.05
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_global_flag = KCW_American_Intervention
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				USA = { has_war_with = ROK }
			}
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -100

		declare_war_on = {
			target = ROK
			type = annex_everything
		}
		
		set_global_flag = KCW_Chinese_Intervention

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.206
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Military Aid Will Suffice"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_global_flag = KCW_American_Intervention
			}
		}
		
		#Symbolizes Chinese Manpower Sent To Korea
		add_manpower = -1450000
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -217500
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = 50
		
		DPK = {
			country_event = {
				id = DNC_Diplomacy.205
				hours = 6
			}
			division_template = {
   				name = "Chinese Troops"
    			is_locked = yes
    			priority = 1
    			template_counter = 0
    			regiments = {
    			    infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
    			    infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
    			    infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
    			    infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
    			}

				#equivalent to 10k soldiers

			}
			
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { num_div = 1 }
				while_loop_effect= {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { num_div < 145}
					}

					create_unit = {
    					division = "name = \"Chinese Troops\" division_template = \"Chinese Troops\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.2"
    					owner = DPK		
					}
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_div = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		set_global_flag = KCW_Chinese_Intervention

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.206
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Better Not Get Involved"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_global_flag = KCW_American_Intervention
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 8
				has_idea = foreign_neutral
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 8
				has_idea = neutrality_idea
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { has_global_flag = KCW_American_Intervention }
			}
		}
		
		add_war_support = -0.10
		add_stability = 0.10
		add_political_power = 100
		set_global_flag = KCW_No_Chinese_Intervention

	}
}

			factor = 10
		}

			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = RI_friendly_foreign_policy
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = RI_friendly_foreign_policy
			target = FROM
		}
		add_manpower = 10200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SOV
			}
			add_manpower = -10200
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = CW_Expansion_country.311
					hours = 6
				}
			}

				id = CW_Expansion_news.311

# Geneva Summit
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.384
	title = CW_Expansion_country.384.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.384.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country384
	fire_only_once = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	tag = SWI
	#	date > 1955.7.18
	#	date < 1956.1.1
	#}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.384.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		add_political_power = 25
		
		#Countries participating in the summit get the event
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					tag = SOV
					tag = FRA
					tag = ENG
					tag = USA
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = CW_Expansion_country.384
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		
		#Countries participating in the summit improve relations with each other
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					tag = SOV
					tag = FRA
					tag = ENG
					tag = USA
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tag = SOV
						tag = FRA
						tag = ENG
						tag = USA
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ron_diplomatic.204
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Switzerland triggers the news event
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SWI 
			}
			news_event = {
				id = CW_Expansion_news.384
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = CW_Expansion_country.386.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country386

		tag = EGY
		date > 1955.8.18
		date < 1956.1.1
		OR = {
			owns_state = 551
			SUD = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		OR = {
			owns_state = 1117
			SSD = {
				is_subject_of = SUD
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			EGY = {
				release = SSD
				end_puppet = SSD
			}
			EGY = {
				release = SUD
				end_puppet = SUD
			}
			SSD = {
				country_event = {
					id = ron_decolonizationdiplo.30
					hours = 6
				}
			}
			SUD = {
				country_event = {
					id = ron_decolonizationdiplo.30
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_country.386.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		SUD = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SSD
				type = civil_war
			}
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.386
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_decolonizationcountry.x.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		SSD = {
			country_event = {
				id = ron_decolonizationdiplo.2
				hours = 1
			}
		}
	}

		}

		name = "Crush Them"

			factor = 10
		}

			AND = {
				has_government = fascism
				has_civil_war = yes
				surrender_progress > 29

		}

		name = CW_Expansion_country.469.a

			factor = 10
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
			add_stability = -0.20
			add_war_support = -0.20
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			add_stability = 0.20
			add_war_support = 0.20
		}
		
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.469
			hours = 6
		}
	}

# US Stratoget Shot Down Over Barents Sea
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.520
	title = CW_Expansion_country.520.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.520.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country520
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		date > 1960.7.1
		date < 1961.1.1
		country_exists = USA
		NOT = { USA = { has_government = communism } }
		has_government = communism
	}

	option = {
		name = "Shoot It Down"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 50

		USA = { 
			country_event = {
				id = ron_diplomatic.520
				hours = 6
			}
		}

		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.520
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Not Needed"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		
	}
}

# King Mahendra Deposes Democratic Government In Nepal
country_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_country.526
	title = CW_Expansion_country.526.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_country.526.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CW_Expansion_country526
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = NEP
		date > 1960.12.15
		date < 1961.6.1
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = neutrality
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			add_timed_idea = { idea = Recent_coup days = 130 } 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				neutrality = 100
			}
		}
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mahendra"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/NEP/CW/Nepal_Mahendra.dds"
			ideology = despotism
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mahendra"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/NEP/CW/Nepal_Mahendra.dds"
			ideology = constitutional_monarchism
		}
		news_event = {
			id = CW_Expansion_news.526
			hours = 6
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ron_coupscountry.x.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = NEP
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Mahendra"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/NEP/CW/Nepal_Mahendra.dds"
						ideology = despotism
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				news_event = {
					id = ron_coupnews.6
					hours = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dimitrov's Death
news_event = {
	id = CW_Expansion_news.529
	title = CW_Expansion_news.529.t
	desc = CW_Expansion_news.529.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_CW_dimitrov_death

	major = yes

	trigger = {
		has_date > 1949.7.2
		BUL = {
			has_country_leader = BUL_georgi_dimitrov
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_news.529.a
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		retire_character = BUL_georgi_dimitrov
		promote_character = BUL_vasil_kolarov 
	}

	option = {
		name = CW_Expansion_news.529.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		retire_character = BUL_georgi_dimitrov
		promote_character = BUL_vasil_kolarov 
	}
}
